The Tick Tock Company Co

2558

6 O'clock Road, halfway...

I have a small computer graveyard in my closet, and I bet I’m not the only one. Do you have an old laptop or keyboard and monitor taking up space? Put it to good use! Imagine blocks of skyscrapers filled with little rooms where people, much like you and I spend most of their waking hours – moving their digits across letters on plastic pads with symbols on them. Our tools are now more advanced, with many flavors of computing, input and output devices, most of which are connected. These devices, and the possibilities they open up, have (with our help of course) developed marvelously diverse ways of subtly thieving away more and more of our time. Any metropolis today represents an ever-evolving symbiosis with technology. Helps us explore this topic on-Playa in 3 easy steps: 1. Bring an old laptop or monitor/keyboard with you to Black Rock City this year. 2. Show up at 7PM on Friday at the halfway point between the Man and Center Camp along the 6 o’clock avenue. 3. We ask that you sit down forming a grid and look busy, typing for 20-25 minutes, We will work with the town of Gerlach to set up techno-trash bins you can use on the way out, or if your device still works after the playa treatment, look into donating it to the Gerlach school district. More details to come, but the core of the idea is really rather simple. Let's do a little exploration of how modern humans spend their time on this planet. Thoughts and ideas, and of course participation are very welcome.

hip hop Open Mic Live

2828

FreeStyle Palace

Part alchemy and part black magic, FreeStyle Palace is an amalgam of sophisticated and authentic Urban Underground music and culture forged by the heat of the Black Rock Desert and polished by the collective talent of Burning Man Participants. We interpret the 2010 Metropolis theme as a tribute and embrace of the Urban Underground experience we have shared with our Burning Man community for the past six years. In his discussion of the Metropolis theme, Larry Harvey must have been thinking about FreeStyle Palace when he described “hubs of social interaction” which “generate the pulse of urban life.” FreeStyle Palace is a “hub” of many cultures, races and generations. We produce a steady “pulse” via amplified kick drum and electronic beat. The “hub” and “pulse” of FreeStyle Palace is a backdrop for Burning Man Participants to create a personal Urban Underground experience like those which radiated from cities both modern and ancient.

Malvoye The Mentalist

2972

Malvoye the Mentalist

Malvoye the Mentalist: A fully automated antique fortune telling booth, bestows versions and visions of the future. Nightly, Malvoye's powers of mentalism are summoned to give YOU your very own unique and astonishingly accurate fortune.  Malvoye knows all, Malvoye sees all.  Seeking love, wealth or the answer to that burning question deep inside you? Each and every reading gives YOU the chance to ask Malvoye your most burning questions. So, come one, come all—put Malvoye to the test! Malvoye's beautiful assistants will instruct you on the proper use of the machine. BUT DO BEWARE, as true fortunes convey more than mere pacifying happiness and positivity.  Now heard in fully restored Vita-phonic sound!  A truly unique experience for the citizens of the playa, this Deco 1930's booth was only just recently restored after nearly being lost to time and the elements. The booth, reportedly once part of a now long defunct traveling sideshow, was famous for its uncanny accuracy and genuine powers. In its day, it was said to be the creation of Edgar Cayce (the "Sleeping Prophet") who was somehow able to imbue his power into the booth. It is also said to be the true inspiration for the Tom Hanks's film Big. It is believed to be one of only five Malvoye booths made and the only one known to have survived. It has been painstakingly rewired and restored by a group of burners in the Philadelphia area who happened upon the booth at a local auction and flea market. ***The booth will only be powered and functioning during the times listed though other random nightly hours will be added, especially around the nights of the burns. PLEASE DO NOT attempt to use the booth during other times as you could easily damage it, respect the set boundaries and do not touch the booth.

4pyre²

3223

4pyre²

4pyre² is a 12ft pipe with propane burners on each end. When the burners fire, the pipe is propelled around on two axes, tracing out the surface of a 12ft diameter sphere. (4πr² is the formula for the surface area of a sphere of radius r.) Enabling this pipe to spin is a gleaming machine of aluminum, stainless steel, bearings, shafts, hoses, rotary fluid unions, sprockets, chains, motors, encoders, and microcontrollers. Standing nearly 18’ tall, it holds the sphere of fire high enough that visitors can get quite close. There is also a panel where visitors can control the angle and the thrust of the propane burners, creating different patterns through the sphere. 4pyre² is a 12ft pipe with propane burners on each end. When the burners fire, the pipe is propelled around on two axes, tracing out the surface of a 12ft diameter sphere. (4πr² is the formula for the surface area of a sphere of radius r.) Enabling this pipe to spin is a gleaming machine of aluminum, stainless steel, bearings, shafts, hoses, rotary fluid unions, sprockets, chains, motors, encoders, and microcontrollers. Standing nearly 18’ tall, it holds the sphere of fire high enough that visitors can get quite close. There is also a panel where visitors can control the angle and the thrust of the propane burners, creating different patterns through the sphere. 4pyre² was designed and built by Christopher Schardt (Spin, Ping, Yantra, Nebula), with major assistance from Peter Luka, Vince Mills, and Russ Zinner.

blackSKYwhite

3348

Dust Circus

Join us in the Dust Circus camp for the shows of blackSKYwhite Aliens Circus from Russia. They will bring citizens of BRC Metropolis to their fantastic planet introducing them to some of the surreal and grotesque entities that belong in realms of darkness. Since 1988 “blackSKYwhite” has been shocking audiences in many famous international shows as Edinburgh Theatrical Festival, London International Mime Festival, Glastonbury Festival and dozens more. Finally this world famous and repeated awarded troupe comes to Burning man in 2010! Their shows illuminate the term 'total theatre': the costumes, scenery, lighting, music and movement blend so seamlessly into a language we all recognize in our deepest emotions and dreams. In this bizarre world there are aliens and creepy crawlies that are fascinating as they twitch and squirm. They are the products of a riotous imagination and we are as enthralled as we are repelled. There is beauty and fear, malice and mischief, magnificent creations jerking and wobbling and shuffling and slithering and bouncing around the stage. It is a dance macabre of feverish rhythms.

PHONOFLaKES live @ Center Camp

3603

Center Camp Cafe

PHONOFLaKES: The best Alternative Rock / Power Pop that Europe has to offer! Sometimes following your instincts is the easiest path to success. PHONOFLaKES from Switzerland, Europe followed this route. The band presents emotional, yet wrenching work, which needs no explanation. With an uncompromising and spontaneous Alternative Rock / Power Pop, their music is a strong and honest impact that gets to you. And it is this strength, expressed through their simple but direct naturalness, which has always been a defining quality of the bands live shows. PHONOFLaKES displays a personality equaled by no other band. Singer Melanie Schweickardt’s exceptional voice puts the band among the greatest Swiss bands – despite the fact they just started working on their debut long player in April 2010. «We made it!» isn’t in the vocabulary of this tireless group. The main goal of PHONOFLaKES is to move ever forward. There’s no doubt what so ever – these guys know what to do and how to do it. In 2009, the band played several shows in San Francisco’s Bay Area, a live radio showcase on KPDO 89.3 pirate cat radio and also performed on the center camp stage at Burning Man 2009. PHONOFLaKES promised to come back to California and Burning Man 2010 and they will give you a night to remember!

Burning Slam! - A Playa Poetry Slam

3658

Couch Burners

Born in Chicago in the 80's, and a far cry from the civilized quiet Tuesday afternoon readings in back corners of libraries that you may have in mind when someone says "poetry", a poetry slam is a rowdy competition where the emphasis is on performance, entertainment and audience participation. Five judges will be placed in the audience and will give you a score out of 10 based on audience reaction. Poets job is to win over the audience. A poem can be whatever you want it to be – a story, a rant, a social commentary, a personal confession. It can be funny, sexy, bizarre, political, truth or complete BS, whatever – provided that you follow a few simple rules, explained below. - Poems must be original material by the person who is performing - Poets get 3 minutes at the microphone. Points deducted for going over time - There will be two rounds. 12 poets in first round, 5 in second - No instruments or props allowed. Costumes should be kept to a minimal - Poems that attack others on basis of race, gender, religion, sexual orientation or any other form of discrimination will not be tolerated and you will be disqualified The event will begin at 5pm on Friday evening at Couch Burners Camp – 5.00 and Florence. This will be a fun event and the audience is encouraged to participate. Feel free to bring shakers, clappers, bells, whistles and other noise makers. So now I am just in need of poets to compete! Step up, bring your mad poetry skills and an attitude and see you if you can walk away with the title of Black Rock City Burning Slam Grand Champion (and hopefully some prizes that I’m trying to source). Send me an email if you’re interested in competing. ajsiggie@gmail.com I’m also in need of judges, so let me know if you would like to involved that way. See you on the Playa, where words become legends. Peace PrairieKiwi

Ken Hamazaki / Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD

3700

at the Man

The art performance by Japanese contemporary artist, Ken Hamazaki. This is the 9th Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- at Burning Man. This performance was inspired by and arranged from the Japanese traditional tea ceremony. The original ceremony consists of a variety of manners to drink, but to experience this fully, please drink with a style you favor most. The most interesting practice would be turning your thought toward him for a few minutes without speaking and enjoy drinking in this small silent space.  I always serve this tea for whoever sits down in front of me. Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- is always a great tool to communicate universally without any thought of hierarchy. I'll be happy if you find any good idea for the future prospect of our metropolis throughout this performance. A big red umbrella will be there as the landmark. GRATEFUL RED! Furthermore, I will exhibit my works and will serve you the tea again in San Francisco after Burning Man. Please join us when you are free. For more detail, please visit the following links.  Ken Hamazaki Red Museum http://www.kenhamazaki.jp NEW PEOPLE http://www.newpeopleworld.com J-POP SUMMIT FESTIVAL http://newpeopleworld.com/j-pop

Nexus Galaxatron

3719

Nexus

The Galaxatron is the power plant of Nexus. It is a 30 foot glowing dome that draws its energy from the Playa through large pyramid conduits that surround the dome (top secret alien technology) that focus this energy into mega conductors that each plug into the dome. These mega conductors are each programmed to show energy flow through thousands of programmed LED’s; and in the heart of this alien machine lays the Tesla Coil. The Tesla Coil will be battles by Koleman, a pro fire performer! You don't wanna miss this. Located at 10 and Esplanade

Amazing radio on 99.1FM, The BRBC

4495

Fandango

The BRBC (99.1FM) is a 100% solar powered FM radio station that brings you the best music you'll hear on the playa. Broadcasting 24/7 from the RadioShaque(tm) in Fandango Village, we play everything from hiphop to oldies and every genre in between! ----- Tired of ultra-supertrance-minimal-megathump-beatbreak-housecore? The BRBC plays a welcome mix of music with instruments such as: DRUMS! GUITARS! PIANOS! VOCALISTS! It's a regular cavalcade of awesome music, played strictly for your listening pleasure. ----- Want to try your hand at being a DJ? Come by the station and play your own jams! We'll show you how to run the board and sound like a real radio professional. Bring your iPod or a CD with MP3s on it and program your own real live radio show. ----- If being on-air isn't your thing, come grab a sticker to show your friends how incredibly cool and cutting edge you are. They'll know who's boss when you're sporting your flashy BRBC schwag! ----- Want to sit around and chuckle with your friends? Get up early-ish and listen to the morning-ish show. Laugh along with our hilarious DJs as we lay out the day's events and relentlessly mock people we disagree with! ----- Stay tuned all day and night to fill your hear-holes with the best stuff since pickles on the playa. ----- Our 7th year broadcasting is going to be our best yet, so don't miss a full week of audio hijinks - tune your radio to 99.1FM and break off the knob. ----- 99.1 FM - The BRBC - Black Rock Broadcasting Corporation - 100% solar powered radio.

Folk Opera Lillian (aboard JUNKraft)

4840

Located at JUNKraft art...

Lillian tells the story of a young man kept awake by the fear that he’s watching his lover, who sleeps soundly in bed, drift away from him, becoming one of the many things he’s lost in his life. He determines that all the things we lose end up in an island of trash floating in the Pacific Ocean and in a desperate attempt to reclaim these things; he sets off on a scuba-diving journey to that island. Along the way he meets strange sea creatures, who trigger discoveries within his mind’s journey to determine how and why he began to lose Lillian. The young man’s desire for love propels him further into the night, and into a swell of events he could never have imagined. JUNKraft is a boat built from 15,000 plastic bottles that sailed across the Pacific Ocean in 2008 to bring attention to the issue of plastic marine pollution. JUNK will be exhibited with a kiosk on plastic pollution built from waste salvaged from Hurricane Katrina. Disposable plastic waste, a byproduct of our ignorance and overconsumption, flows from land to sea through rivers and storm drains, getting stuck in massive, oceanic current systems called "gyres". Plastic accumulates in the gyres, breaking down into smaller and smaller fragments that are eaten by marine organisms. How might this affect human health? We have a story to tell about a better future, and want to begin by bringing this message to Black Rock City, through a resurrection of the JUNK

Ayla Nereo Accoustic Set

4871

Department of Tethered ...

Ayla Nereo sings her lyrical folk music, weaving words and infectious melodies into a cocoon of brilliant light and cozy atmosphere. It will sink you deeply into your self, and lift your heart wide open. Ayla Nereo came from the hills of Sonoma County, a child grown on blackberries and books. The lines of vision and waves of hearing brushed her shoulder one day, and it started to come out as music.Some say it sounds like Joni Mitchell and Buffy Saint-Marie having tea with Feist. Some say it’s like teleportation into the mind’s eye of what could be, if we choose it. Some dance. Hear for yourself.Keep an eye to the sky and an ear to the sounds around… There is a revolution of conscious hearing, a casting-off of bitter judgment, and it’s in your eyes…

Sunset Temple Earth Harp Performance

4933

The Temple of Transitio...

MASS Ensemble's Artistic Director, William Close, and Associate Director, Andrea Brook, welcome you home as they transform the Temple of Transition into a magical, musical instrument. MASS (Music, Architecture, Sonic, Sculpture) Ensemble’s extraordinary Earth Harp is the world’s largest stringed instrument, placing the audience inside the instrument, as the golden strings span out from the stage and use the Temple of Transition to create a 120 foot harp. MASS Ensemble is an internationally renowned performing arts group that combines unique musical sculptures and installations with traditional instrumentation, creating an unforgettable multi-sensory experience. Immediately following the Sunset performances, the audience is welcome to play The Earth Harp!

Trojan Horse Grand Procession, Party, & Burn

4940

Trojan Horse

Before sundown on the fifth night of Burning Man, the Trojan Horse will begin its last “rights” of passage. Columns of Burners will pull the 20-ton beast on its massive cart across the playa and through the Gates of Troy to where the beast will burn. A large procession with loud, cacophonic music will accompany the migration. The music, composed by Douglas Bevans, will be interactive and performed by a massive corps of drummers and brass players. The procession of costumed Greek deities and Greek and Trojan mortals will be solemn, the death march and last rites for the horse. We believe this will be one of the largest and most spectacular pieces of performance art ever brought to the playa. Once the horse passes through the Gates of Troy, pure pandemonium (led by Pan) and a full-scale celebration with DJs and a powerful sound system will erupt. At midnight Artemis, Apollo, and their band of archers will shoot flaming arrows onto the upper reaches of the beast. Zor the Fyre God will finish torching the horse. In a spectacular conflagration, the horse will burn quickly and the party and dancing will resume around the fallen beams and embers. A riotous night of revelry (some orchestrated) will follow. Dionysius reigns!

To Grahama's House We Go!

4981

Elephant Bird Camp

Elephant Bird Camp presents Grahama’s House, a scaled-down and mobile version of your suburban grandma’s house. The exterior has all the visual cues, from the shingled roof, to the paneled siding, shuttered windows, etc. The inside is furnished with vintage furniture, 50’s wallpaper, elegant light fixtures, hardwood flooring, and hilarious photos from “Grahama’s” life on the walls. A working ceiling fan will cool the guests while they eat hard candy and experience the creature comforts of plastic covered sofas and creepy pictures from Grahama’s life. As a bonus, an actual “Grahama” will guilt trip you about your naughtiness and simultaneously make you feel like the specialist little boy/girl. It’s as if your real grahama were on the playa with you! To celebrate her first year on playa we are having an all night party with live bands perched atop the roof! Granny may be old, but she knows how to party!

"So You Wanna Be A DJ" Shock Collar Gong Show

5011

Want It!

Have you always dreamed of throwing down a legendary DJ set at one of the hottest camps on the playa? Well, how bad do you Want It? We've got 10,000 watts of juicy sound, some of the best real estate in Black Rock City, and a nighttime crowd just waiting to be whipped into a frenzy. All you have to do is wow our panel of judges and you too could be headlining Burning Man! For this contest we hearken back to that seminal masterpiece of talent programs: The Gong Show. Perhaps you remember the cringe-worthy showcase of questionable performances that critics could halt by striking a loud gong. This event is eerily similar, only ours has balls. Ovaries too. Giant, dusty gonads. Can you hang? Instead of a gong, DJs will wear a shock collar and get buzzed off stage by volts of harsh rejection if they fail to impress. Instead of regaling us with tap dancing, DJs break out their most mind blowing tracks and slickest tricks. Instead of a paltry sum to commemorate victory, winners will be invited back during peak hours to pound the dance floor into submission. This is open decks for the fearless. Bring it.

Open Mic/Poetry Slam -CS!

5213

Couch Burner Camp

Born in Chicago in the 80's, and a far cry from the civilized quiet Tuesday afternoon readings in back corners of libraries that you may have in mind when someone says "poetry", a poetry slam is a rowdy competition where the emphasis is on performance, entertainment and audience participation. This is also an open mic to show off your creative side. Song? Dance? Performance? Bring it. There will be sign up sheets at the campsite prior to the event day for you to join in. If you're late for your slot, we'll go down the line, and you can re-add yourself to the end if there's room. All are welcome to join in on the fun, contributing your creativity, or just sitting back to enjoy the show. If we have a good showing and interest, we may just repeat the event later on in the week.

Hechi-ken Hamazaki / Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD

5227

Playawaste Raiders

The art performance by Japanese contemporary artist, Ken Hamazaki. This is the 12th Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- at Burning Man. This performance was inspired by and arranged from the Japanese traditional tea ceremony. The original ceremony consists of a variety of manners to drink, but to experience this fully, please drink with a style you favor most. The most interesting practice would be turning your thought toward him for a few minutes without speaking and enjoy drinking in this small silent space. I always serve this tea for whoever sits down in front of me. Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- is always a great tool to communicate universally without any thought of hierarchy. I'll be happy if we could find any great idea to make better and more enjoyable future throughout this tea ceremony. Furthermore, I will do something interesting in San Francisco before Burning Man this year. Please join us if you have time before you head to the playa For more detail, please visit the following links. Ken Hamazaki Red Museum http://www.kenhamazaki.jp/

5339

DISORIENT

Miss Black Rock City Pageant 2011: Call for Participation!! When: Friday, 2-4pm (contestants arrive 1 hour before to register) Where: DISORIENT What: Represent your city, your camp, your art, your tent, or just yourself! Participants (open to all shes, zes, and hes) are to arrive 1 hour prior to the pageant and will reveal their unique inner beauty in 3 categories: 1) The One Minute (no)Talent Competition: No rules, everyone has a talent - be it a stupid party trick or a fine art! 2) Interview: Do they do it for world peace, the children, or for the puppies? 3) Fashion: Show us your personal playa Style! All participants are beautiful and everyone wins by participating. Please come with a sash (be a "Miss" something as we are all a lil amiss) and a tiara. Hosted by Miss Everything to Infinity-Ali Luminescent! NOTE: No Beauty pageant is fair, bribing the "judges" and your host is encouraged. Participate for fun, rather than playing to win! The MBRC Project produced events on-playa, around the USA, the UK and Spain since 2004. Tsunami Bass Experience ~津波低音経験~ Wobble tha ~WaVe~

5522

Tsunami Bass Experience...

Looking for music? Then wobble on over to the 20ft TSUNAMI ~WaVe~ installation located towards 10 o'clock and Tokyo for a unique BASS immersion EXPERIENCE like no other. Upon completion of multiple rites of passage, The Tsunami Bass Experience's Morphous & ShiZaru present the ~WaVe~ Version 7.0~!! for the express purpose of enlightenment edutainment and the facilitation of proper bass culture appreciation as our collective gift to playa BM 2011. The ~WaVe~ installation, which debuted in NYC in Feb 2011, is a unique sound system, capable of generating low frequencies down to 5Hz, providing the ultimate in BASS CULTURE appreciation. "How LOW can u GO?!?" And just like the Tsunami Bass Experience you know and love in NYC, we will be hosting an amazing line-up of the best in local, domestic & international bass culture talent including the familar residents & guests u love, as well as new to the ~WaVe~ bass masters in their virgin appearences. For full details on the daily line-up and more, go to: www.tsunamibassexperience.com under EVENTS or check our FACEBOOK page. ~"Come on in, the BASS is fine, and we be swimmin' in it"~ "Brace Urself, as the BASS hits ya, DuBtRiPfLiPfAnTaSiA~!!"

World's Largest Synchronized Swim!

5808

The Pier

We'll be performing near "The Pier" art installation on Thursday at 4pm. Those who arrive first will begin a spiral formation and those who join in will keep adding themselves to the spiral. Danyavaad and The Shimmy Sisters

5865

Sacred Spaces Village

Danyavaad and the Shimmy Sisters invite you to embark on a cultural journey through dance, music and the mystique of the East. Gypsy World Rock and Eclectic Bellydancing. “I saw you all at Wanderlust and WOW, amazing performance. The ancient Bards and Muses were frolicking in the etherworlds above and below you in unison to your performance.” - John Marosi “My expectations were exceeded! The Shimmy Sisters combined with Danyavaad, make up what is by far the best Middle Eastern influenced ensemble I have ever experienced.” - San Diego Beach Life Magazine “A Spiritually Rockin Journey! The full house included everyone from your all American dad with his two 10 year old daughters, to Burners and internationally known dancers, to local musicians. With standing room only, people sat on the floor, and stood between tables and chairs and by the end, the entire crowd was dancing along with them! A man in the audience said ‘it feels like I am being taken back into an ancient past ... into my nomadic past life.’ ”- The Papyrus “Everyone was mesmerized by the sight. On stage, the beautiful Shimmy Sisters bellydanced and balanced long, sleek swords on their heads while leaning back into a somewhat contorted position. The members of Danyavaad closed their eyes and sank into the Middle Eastern-fusion music they were making, and with the skilled DJ Sandbag on bass, Gabriel Penix on dumbek and Greg Vaughan on electric sitar.” - Kinsee Morlan of the San Diego CityBeat “The Shimmy Sisters and Danyavaad captivated the crowd with enticing movements set to hypnotic rhythms. The belly-dancing Shimmy Sisters produced a stunning visual delight with twirling skirts intermingling with multiple colored scarves to become living, moving art. The sisters’ concentration, flexibility and control were evident as they, with flaming swords balance on their heads, stretched and twisted eliciting applause from the audience.“ - Elizabeth Guiten of the Imperial Beach Eagle & Times

Tibetan Sound and Gong Healing

5875

Chakralicious Camp

Utilizing the sounds and vibrations of Tibetan singing bowls, gongs and chimes we are able to relax into a deep state of meditation allowing ourselves to heal and re-align. These ancient sounds bring our body, mind and spirit into its’ natural resonant frequency. Vibrations are able to pass through our body, removing internal clutter and allowing our minds to clear from the constant chatter. The relaxing tones invoke blissful enlightened states and sensations of weightlessness, opening, flying and floating.

Brian Travis

5878

Chakralicious Camp

"It’s not every day that a club owner sets his bar on fire to celebrate a great performance from a visiting band, but that’s just what happened when The BTB rocked the Isla Cantina. As the band dove into the Burning Man-themed crowd favorite “Gasoline,” a row of flame whipped across the top of the bar. “We were firing on all cylinders that night,” says singer & guitarist Brian Travis. “The place was packed & we were charged up. Our best shows don’t just rely on execution. They happen when we’re playing with great energy and the kind of momentum that pushes rock 'n roll forward, tapping into the spirit of the music itself.” Travis, Mark Wickliffe (drums) & Steve Wiel (bass) effortlessly mix classic rock with twangs of country & hints of the blues, giving traditional folk melodies a unique rock and roll vibe. With 5 albums of original content released, the core group of Travis, Wickliffe & Wiel continues to wow Los Angeles crowds with their own brand of heartfelt rock n roll. “The BTB show is real,” says Wiel. ” There is nothing staged, nothing scripted, hell, sometimes we don’t even have a setlist. Each show is like no other & you never know what’s going to happen.” The BTB has worked hard to earn its place as a Los Angeles mainstay, & with plans for future material & an upcoming tour already in the works, the band won’t be taking a break anytime soon. There is simply too much burning passion in the band’s driven frontman. “We’re exploring all these different sides of ourselves right now,” Travis explains. “We’re planning to record an album with the country sound we’ve been exploring lately. But after that, we’re going to get back to the rock stuff– because that’s truly what’s in my heart.” - Erin Johnson, June 2010

“Songs of the Hearts on Fire”

6513

Serenity Giant Game Cam...

A performance piece towards the experience of a collaborative action painting. A large canvas is set on the ﬂoor, as a stage. It is an invitation to dance with paint. To ground the experience into the canvas with sweat and laughing feet. Two performance pieces, one hour each. After the event, the canvas is laid out to dry, cut up in pieces and showcased at the camp. Each piece is marked with the title of the song, a quote, and a technical note. A follow-up party is intended to give out a piece of the painting to all of the participants. David Black and Elizabeth Romo.

Gabriel Gilmore

6983

Sacred Spaces Village

The Journey - Life Cycle Evolution The first blurry ebbs & flows of life in protective space, growing with the beat of our initial life source. Painfully but beautifully, our space transforms & we enter the world. A tremendous, grounding grandeur marks our arrival & the rhythm of life begins. As we seek expression, understanding & movement, we drift in an emotional but transient phase & succumb to the flow of life. Eventually we discover our 'voice' & finding contentment in the language of music, our simultaneous sameness & uniqueness is revealed. Seeking transcendence, we push the boundaries of experience, towards the inevitable & incredible transformation which marks the often sombre, but ultimately celebratory end/beginning.

Song, Dust, Sing: Singer Songwriter Open Showcase

7131

Reverbia: All Live Musi...

Song, Dust, Sing...hosted by Reverbia (All Live Music Camp)...provides the setting for one of the most popular open mic, singer/songwriter showcases happening in Black Rock City. Each day, 14-16 Artists will usually ride in from the desert, with instrument on their back and dust on their boots, hoping to scribe their name for one of the few cherished slots available at this unique, 2 song and out, 90 minute long...singer/songwriter showcase. Expectations are soon fulfilled for both the large attentive audience and the performing artist...as the sound system amplifies quality and the Reverbia Embassy Shade Structure provides the necessary cool space...to evoke chilled out vibes, for a long hot afternoon. Visit us once, twice, or everyday for this unique sampler of singer/songwriter talent...and support Live Music at Burning Man.

You're The Limit Stage

7163

Above The Limit

Camp Above The Limit is hosting an open mic Musicians' Happy Hour Monday thru Thursday from 4:00 pm till 8:00 pm with a grand performance on Saturday. We will have scheduled and ad hoc performances promoting musical diversity, radical self expression, participation, and entertainment. If you are a musician or performance artist and wish to play on the "You're The Limit Stage" bring yourself, your talent and your instrument to Camp Above The Limit and participate in our Musical Diversity Program! It doesn't matter what it is! From violin to kazoo, guitar to ocarina, banjo, sarod, sitar, Spanish bagpipes, heck even accordions are welcome. Bluegrass, Shamanic, Old Timey, Country, Rock, Classical, Irish, English, Morris Dancing, French, Middle Eastern, Balkan, Afghan, Indian, Barber Shop, or performance art. Whether it be your whole band or your radically self-expressive solo act, bring it! We will provide sound and we'll have other musicians for accompaniment: drums, guitar, mandolin, most likely anything you would need. We will be putting together an all-star performance on Saturday for all those who participate so come be a part of a great community of musicians and performance artists and share your gifts with us and the playa! Community is what makes the Burn so great and within all communities there is greatness! Come share yours with all of us!

Green Foot Glass Camp

7173

Green Foot Glass Camp

Glass Camp is a highly interactive project. Glass blowing is a mesmerizing art in itself. While it’s an art form dating backing to the birth of humanity, it’s still relatively new in the United States. The glow of a molten, honey-like material at night is hypnotic. The radiant heat of the equipment illuminating the hot shop floor is an installation in itself. Glass is a dance, with each team developing its own choreography. We intend to include the audience with ‘You Name It, We Make It’ activities. People can submit a design and our collection of talented artists will assemble what was not thought possible. Our team consists of some of the most skilled emerging and established artists in Seattle, the mecca for glass working in the world. Each night the team will take at least 2 complex designs from the audience and take the 2-D drawing and pull the 3-D design from the hot glass. There is no limit to what can be achieved in glass, and that’s what we intend to show. Glass blowing began in the Fertile Crescent and we hope to take it to Fertility 2.0. These professional artists are encyclopedias of information to anything relating to glass and high temperatures. With the making of glass, questions always arise, and we are equipped with the information to help people understand. All of our equipment was handmade by Evan Schuass, and was used last year in the Keyhole. Mobile glass studios are an excellent display of design, function, and efficiently. He has been commissioned from people all over the West Coast, and Hawaii to build these mobile shops. All the people included in Glass Camp are either producing artists or assistants to the highest level of glass workers in the world. We would like to share our gift and knowledge with the people of Burning Man. Everyone in this camp is here because they have a passion for glass art.

Hang Music by Yogi Prateado

7497

Chakralicious Camp

Yogi Prateado travels the noosphere with the Hang, percussion, electronics, and other devices to woo harmonious realization. The Hang, a U.F.O. looking instrument, was created in 2000, by Felix and Sabina, the Hang makers, in Bern, Switzerland. This remarkable instrument sounds like the celestial orbs, a harp, or what have you. As the primary instrument of sonic creation for Prateado, collaboration with some of the top live and electronic artists on the west coast bring an array of listening and movement experiences. Prateado is currently based in Los Angeles, though finds home anywhere in the world, especially San Francisco, Berlin, and Rio de Janeiro.

Tribe Talks

7761

Red Lightning

TribeTalks is a dynamic venue that enables participants to offer wisdom offerings to the community within a casual, cafe-like environment. Each talk is offered within 3-10 minutes, providing a efficient way to share and enable co-creation and connections. No powerpoint presentations or projections. A dedicated team of partners host, organize, gather information, film, catalog, and share the presentations to our online networks for further co-creation opportunit. The vision is to build a living, open, online forum and resource for participants to have their voices heard and visions seen by our global human family!http://www.youtube.com/TribeTalksOffered and coordinated by Bridgewalkers and The Convergence Networkhttp://www.bridgewalkers.comhttp://theconvergencenetwork.org/

The Salon at Summer Camp Sync. @ Sundown

7764

Summer Camp Sync

A smorgasbord of performance art, music, and spoken word. Bring your  5 -10 min performance to share. Or participate in the Battle of Words hip hop and spoken word slam down. Come early if you have special tech requests. On Playa collaborations and works in progress encouraged. Bear Margaritas for all!! The Salon is a night of creative expression. Our community started hosting salons in January 2010 as a safe space for the folks of Synchronicity and our friends to share finished or unfinished works of art, poetry, song, or any form of creative release. The idea was to encourage people in the community to create, share, and hear thoughts or ideas from fellow creative souls. It has since expanded, and we have enjoyed works of musicians, poets, storytellers, palindromists, historians, novelists, ramblers, gamblers, painters, filmmakers, drunks, fathers, mothers, lovers, dreamers, and psychedelic clowns from all over this land! A crowd of lovely folks from across the playa will be gathering at 7.30 pm in preparation for the night's event. A list will be roaming around, with 20 spots to fill. As 8 pm nears, we pile in front of our stage and are greeted by the lovely host of the evening. From there.. anything goes!

THRIVE Screening/Dialogue with Foster Gamble

7798

Red Lightning

In our 60ft dome, THRIVE creator Foster Gamble will screen his revolutionary film and host an inspired dialogue after the screening. THRIVE is an unconventional documentary that lifts the veil on what's REALLY going on in our world by following the money upstream -- uncovering the global consolidation of power in nearly every aspect of our lives. Weaving together breakthroughs in science, consciousness and activism, THRIVE offers real solutions, empowering us with unprecedented and bold strategies for reclaiming our lives and our future. INTERVIEWS in THRIVE Duane Elgin, Nassim Haramein, Steven Greer, Jack Kasher, Daniel Sheehan, Adam Trombly, Brian O'Leary, Vandana Shiva, John Gatto, Deepak Chopra, David Icke, Catherine Austin Fitts, G. Edward Griffin, Bill Still, John Perkins, Aqeela Sherrills, Evon Peter, Angel Kyodo Williams, Elisabet Sahtouris, Amy Goodman, and Barbara Marx Hubbard.

Actoroke (Karaoke for actors)

7925

Baggage Check

Instead of singing popular songs in front of a live audience, act out scenes from popular movies! What kind of movies? Romances, of course! Here’s how it works: come by and just watch if you like. Then if you decide you’d like to participate throw your name into one or more of the following hats: “straight male, straight female, gay male, or lesbian female.” When it’s time for a new scene we will decide whether it’s straight, gay, or lesbian (based on interest) and draw two names out of the appropriate hat(s) to determine who from the audience will play the two romantic leads. Then we will view a scene from a romance movie, “the kiss”, the scene in the movie where the leads “connect.” After viewing this scene, our Baggage Check film director will direct the two randomly selected volunteers from the audience in recreating this scene, acting out the roles of the romantic leads, while our film crew captures the moment. For example, we might announce that the next scene will be a straight scene and we'd draw names from the straight male and straight female hats. Then we'd announce the movie as, for example, African Queen, and the man and woman selected would play the roles of Humphrey Bogart and Kathrine Hepburn. We would watch the scene on the boat when they've just successfully run the rapids and they kiss for the first time. Then the chosen actors would act out that scene. Then while we repeat this process for more scenes we will edit the results of earlier scenes so that we can view them later in the evening, as they are edited.

Dark Sparkle Burlesque show

7928

Dark Sparkle

Dark Sparkle is the potent mix of the mysterious and the dangerous that makes something irresistibly attractive. It's what pushes people to the point of insanity; that unexplainable quality that pulls people to the dark side. Some days, Dark Sparkle is your alter-ego; other days it is your most natural feeling form. Dark Sparkle is Mona Lisa's smile, biscuits and gravy, the Fonz, the apocalypse. It is an adventurous way of life--physically, emotionally and mentally that citizens of BRC embrace. Our shows are an opportunity for Dark Sparklers and other BRC citizens to explore and showcase their Dark Sparkle through performance, storytelling, and tease. Featuring Nicki Sparxx! Father Figure! Roxy Pop! La Chispa! Red Siren! StraighNasty! and many more. We'll also turn the tables with ample opportunity for participation.

LIVE ROCK MUSIC

7951

Star Star Roadhouse @ B...

Real, live music from kick ass rockers. Thursday-Saturday, 4-7P & 9P-12A. "Life is too damn short for crappy music." Come dance your ass off with Greg and Doug, the organic jukebox duo from the Great White North. These guys know rock: with a mental catalogue of over 3,000 tracks, they can move the crowd like Jagger. Star Star Roadhouse is a destination… a local joint for wayward Burners looking for something different. Here you can catch a live show: classic rock, moody blues or bluegrass… a rare experience at Burning Man. The sound system will be modest: what you'd expect to find at a honky tonk venue with live music. Shows will be twice daily from 4-7, and 9-midnight, with an occasional after hours exception. We will be collaborating with many promoters on playa to book a variety of live bands. Yoga & dance classes will also be offered. The stage will be decked out in classic Americana and vintage California-Nevada highway stylings, with colorful lighting, a sun bleached facade, shaded dance floor and lounge area with comfortable seating. Billiards and darts provide additional play and other interactive games are in the plans. For added excitement and a visually stunning art experience, Artist Jamie Vaida & Crew are building the Fertility Twin mutant vehicles with indirect LED lighting, flame effects, and audio. They will either be parked near the stage or out rocking the playa with classic tunes transporting participants physically and musically. We believe that the live music experience is unique and often absent at Burning Man and “Star Star Roadhouse” would be thrilled to offer it to the community.

Pinata's Revenge

7962

Treepod & Pinata's Reve...

PIÑATA'S REVENGE is a moving interactive performance in which a 'Living Piñata' (a person in an elaborate Piñata costume) is suspended from a large moving boom above our Art Car, the PiñataMobile. One at a time, individuals will be allowed to engage the Piñata in traditional piñata-combat--involving padded bats. Just as with a traditional piñata, if people strike the 'Living Piñata's body hard enough, treasures will 'bleed' forth. But unlike a traditional piñata, people will have to strike with care, because THIS TIME the Piñata will ALSO be armed with a padded bat--with which to exact its revenge! Behold--PIÑATA'S REVENGE!

Play: "After Revolution"

8184

Esplanade

A Site-Specific Play for The Playa. A washed-up barren land where nothing grows, where all is arid and plain. Not a morsel to eat or a drop to be drunk. A scurvy crew of renegades have survived but what is their fate? Surely some revelation is at hand; Surely the Second Coming is at hand. Join us on our theatrical journey to the New World. Look out for the white mast of the SS Serpent Queen, steaming across the esplanade from sundown, Thursday. Come to Camp 2.45 and Jasmine for showtimes. There will also be a secret 4am matinee performance.

Replay Cafe: Fresh Feedback Your Way

8215

3 o'clock and K plaza

Every day we receive feedback from friends, family, lovers, co-workers. Whether the feedback is relatively minor (after dinner a friend mentions that you've left a tip that is too small) to major (a parent expresses disapproval with your choice of partner), it often takes us by surprise. At some point, we've probably all wished we had reacted differently in a feedback situation. To get a do-over, a second chance, a fresh start - a replay! And now you can! Stop by and choose from our menu of feedback scenarios. We'll act out the scene, then you're invited to imagine alternative strategies to improve the experience for the feedback giver or receiver. Join us on stage to put your ideas in action, or give us instructions for the replay. At our Replay Cafe, we serve fresh feedback your way!

Naked Comedy Showcase

8272

Automatic Subconscious

The Naked Comedy Showcase is the creation of Andy Ofiesh, a stand-up comedian from Boston, Massachusetts. For years Andy has organized hosted naked comedy shows featuring Boston area comics doing stand-up in the nude. Andy's first naked comedy show in a public venue was at Improv Boston this past summer days before going to the Edinburgh Fringe in August. News of the event spread quickly and preceded his arrival in Edinburgh. "A group of American comics have performed what could be the world's first naked stand-up show. The little-publicised event in Boston on Tuesday night was a sell-out." — Chortle After arriving in Scotland for the Edinburgh Festival Fringe, Andy seized an opportunity at Spank!, the late night comedy showcase at Smirnoff Underbelly, to do a 1 minute naked promo for the show that he was performing in called Why Work?. The overwhelming positive response at the event prompted Andy to host his Naked Comedy Showcase in Edinburgh. Encouraged by the success of the shows at Improv Boston and at The Fringe in Edinburgh, Andy has organized an ongoing monthly naked comedy show at Improv Boston. News of the show was reported in both of Boston's major newspapers: "Once a month, [Andy] does onstage what most of us could only imagine in our worst nightmare: naked stand-up-comedy...What's more astonishing is that Ofiesh has persuaded other performers to try nude stand-up, too, and now hosts "the Naked Comedy Showcase" at Improv Boston the First Wednesday of every month." — Nick Zaino, Boston Globe "Spectators who appreciated the comedy seemed to outnumber those who may have simply wanted to see naked people." — Sean L McCarthy, Boston Herald Now for the first time the Naked Comedy Showcase can be seen at Burning Man!!!

48 Hour Film Project Kickoff: Black Rock City

8276

Videogasm

The 48 Hour Film Project is a wild opportunity in which you and a team make a movie—write, shoot, edit and score it—in just 48 hours. At the kickoff, you get a character, a prop, a line of dialogue, and a genre, all to include in your movie. 48 hours later, the movie must be complete. Then it will be shown at our "On the Red Carpet Premiere" on Thursday evening, August 30th at 11 PM at our Playa Theater (with an Encore Show on Friday, August 31st at 10 PM). If you have a team and equipment, start at your leisure and follow the instructions on posters found at PlayaInfo and Videogasm (in Snowflake Village). If you want to get people for your team or join a team, come on down to Videogasm at 8:15 and Edelweiss in Snowflake Village on Tuesday at 3pm. The 48 Hour Film Project's mission is to advance filmmaking and promote filmmakers. Through its festivals the Project encourages filmmakers and would-be filmmakers to get out there and make movies. The tight deadline of 48 hours puts the focus squarely on the filmmakers—emphasizing creativity and teamwork skills. While the time limit places an unusual restriction on the filmmakers, it is also liberating by putting an emphasis on "doing" instead of "talking."Note: Anyone making a video must first fill out a personal use form and get a camera tag from Media Mecca in Center Camp.

Encore Show: 48 Hour Film Project BRCity 2012

8278

Videogasm

If you couldn't make it to the (On the Red Carpet) Premiere Show on Thursday, August 30th at 11 PM of the 48 Hour Film Project or are jonesin' for another Playa Videogasm adventure, come to the Friday Encore Show to see the results of the Black Rock City 48 Hour Film Project! Each of these movies was made in 48 hours on the Playa. "Cinderplaya" features a wizard searching for his playa love. "Portaman" discovers a mastermind's plan to destroy Burningman. "Sister Lucy" helps burners learn about sex. During "Abandon All Hope and Fear", a dream teaches the way of the playa. More movies will be included. The 48 Hour Film Project's mission is to advance filmmaking and promote filmmakers. Through its festivals the Project encourages filmmakers and would-be filmmakers to get out there and make movies. The tight deadline of 48 hours puts the focus squarely on the filmmakers—emphasizing creativity and teamwork skills. Hechi-Ken Hamazaki Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD-

8315

Black Rock Army

The art performance by Japanese contemporary artist, Ken Hamazaki. This is the 14th Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- at Burning Man. This performance was inspired by and arranged from the Japanese traditional tea ceremony. The original ceremony consists of a variety of manners to drink, but to experience this fully, please simply drink with a style you favor most. The most interesting practice would be turning your thought toward him for a few minutes without speaking and enjoy drinking in this small silent space. I always serve this tea for whoever sits down in front of me. Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- is always a great tool to communicate universally without any thought of hierarchy. I'll be happy if we could find any great idea to make better and more enjoyable future throughout this tea ceremony. Furthermore, I will do something interesting in San Francisco before Burning Man this year. Please join us if you have time before you are headed for the playa For more detail, please visit the following links. Ken Hamazaki Red Museum http://www.kenhamazaki.jp/

Tsunami Bass Experience

8829

Tsunami Bass Experience...

Come by for a refreshing dip in the multi-sensory waves we will be deluging once again at Camp Tsunami Bass Experience, located at 10 o'clock & deep playa. For our third incarnation the TBE~WaVe~ installation, our body~sonic dance platforms that afford participants a uniquely interactive experience to engage kinesthetically with the music, we are upping the visual ante with the addition of a 30ft. dome to our public frontage. This structure, which will be combined with our wave sculpture, will be curated by the visualist CINEMOEBA, who, as per his 2012 work, will once again be providing a wonderland of analog feedback & other projected delights. This in combination with our live fusion and Dubstep centric line-up featuring some of the finest bass culture talent available on playa, denizens of Black Rock City can expect a fourth dimensional EXPERIENCE like no other. Come wobble the TBE~WaVe~ and challenge your perceptions of bass culture music from every learning and thinking modality. Discover the optimal conditions for proper bass culture appreciation, the facilitation of which is our primary mission. We are devoted to ensuring the Tsunami Bass well~spring of proper bass culture on playa is properly nurtured and celebrated at Burning Man. As the TBE Multiversity of Bass Culture Appreciation founders will preach, proper edutainment is our main goal. We invite you to open your heart/mind and try a new "substance over style" attuned environment, carefully curated by bass culture artists (Established by the Tsunami Bass Experience's Morphous & ShiZaru) for artists & aficionados. This is not a "nightclub on playa" but rather a welcome respite for those seeking low-end frequency with the utmost decency... join us for a more intimate and holistically immersive esthetic environment in which you will experience a full range of frequencies, with the decibels enlightenly engineered properly. Line-up will be posted to the internets so find us!! ~Cheers!~}*{~ (BYOB, NO MOOP)

SHIFT Performance

9534

SHIFT

ZOR has traveled extensively throughout North America, the Caribbean, South Pacific and Europe studying and performing the Fire arts. By incorporating martial arts and dance he has created an exotic one man fire show that is breathtaking and immediately captivates and inspires the audience with its beauty, reverence and showmanship. He now performs for circus acts, parties, nightclubs, weddings, children's camps, team building firewalks, and city sponsored events. Recent works include opening night parties for the prestigious Cirque du Soleil, the official FireConclave performances of Burning Man, and appearances in Rolling Stone, Smithsonian and New Yorker. Sara Huntley Firedancing since 2007, dynamic and inspired, specializing in poi, fans, and double staffs. Currently piloting her brainchild troupe Lux Natura, Sara has been a member of Nocternal Sunshine, Kinetica, and Flux. She has graced many festivals with her performances and workshops, including Burning Man, Fractal Nation, Firedrums, and the SF Fire Arts Expo. http://sarahuntley.weebly.com/

A Capella Chorus Jam

9741

Cartoon Commune

Like to sing? Come to our vocal jam. Last year, we had a blast when a spontaneous chorus broke out in our camp, covering classic harmony-rich songs like Billy Joel's "For the Longest Time," and a tradition was born. We will gather and sing popular, well-known, or timeless songs in harmony (e.g., folk, pop, rock, opera, blues, barbershop, and on and on), without accompaniment (i.e., a capella). Song (lyric) sheets will be provided. All are welcome - no training needed.

Playa Sock Exchange

10014

Silicon Village

The bell has rung and the pandemonium has hit the playa running. Don’t get stuck holding an unpaired sock from when your washer or dryer claimed the other half. Bring them to the Playa Sock Exchange (PSE) for a half hour of crazy sock trading. However, unlike Wall Street we ask that you don’t air your dirty laundry here, please bring clean socks (a little dusty is fine, just not stinky). You may bring singles or pairs and trade up or down with fellow traders. There will be a limited supply of IPO seed sock available for you to choose from if you find you are shorted of socks on arrival. Trade once, trade twice, trade as many times as you want. Trading ends when the final bell rings. Everyone comes out ahead, or afoot as the case may be.

Reverbia: All Live Musi...

Wisdom hosted 2013 Reggae on the River and has been performing on Main Stages at festivals across the West Coast. DJ Solrising is the former US Scratching Champion. Also performing at 8:45pm, Buckman Coe will be performing a new solo looping set. Buckman's band was voted 2013 Best Band in Vancouver, BC. and Buckman has also played at many festivals across Canada and the West Coast US. Opening the night will be Shovelman. The well known sound looper who plays a shovel that is stringed like a guitar. Shovelman is a favorite on the US festival circuit and will set the tone for this great evening of talent at Reverbia's Urban Night Concerts.

Eye of Argon Reinactment

10164

Silicon Village

Participants will gather near the stage to take turns reading this terrible short story in all of its glory and flaws. A person reads until either 1) they finish one page or they laugh. Once this happens the script is then passed along to the next reader. Meanwhile participants will be on stage with a variety of props that we provide (or those which are brought) and act out the scenes, however improbable, on stage. You’ll laugh, you’ll cry, you’ll kiss a little of your time in BRC goodbye! Please note there is dialogue of a crude nature which while not vulgar may not be appropriate for very young audience members, but then again even adults who hear it may be confused. Join us at the Thirsty Camel Stage.

Bobby Wheelock Funpack delivery party

10417

Every intersection on L...

Bobby Wheelock needs 32 volunteers to help deliver the Funpack flyers to every burning man participant. Deliver 2000 flyers and get much schwagg. ------- Yes, Bobby Wheelock has finally worked out how to give back to every participant on the playa. This will encompass delivering 64,000 unique flyers to everyone. And we need YOU to help. -------- Upon taking this great privilege, you will zig zag down the streets and give flyers to all participants - and these are not your normal flyers. Each one is different, unique, and special. There are jokes, puzzles, games, gags, and coupons, and ultimately a higher purpose - to make sure every burner gets the true value of decommodification. These flyers are also very well organized so as to tell participants everything they need to know - their new Playa name, color, home planet and more! ------ To participate, Please wait at your most convenient corner on the outlying road of Laissez-faire on wednesday morning, and look for the mutant vehicle with a big Z on it. We will provide you with a bag full of a chunk of flyers, a map with directions, a official postal cap, and a second bag so you can collect all the gifts that are Deserved to you by the populace of Burning Man for your amazing volunteer effort. The routes will be back and forth from each 1/2 hour street, moving inward from Laissez-faire to the Esplanade. ------ Help us with this amazing performance art project. Help us ensure that Decommodification stays as a true principal! ------ Who is Bobby Wheelock? Bobby is one of the earliest human clones. Born in 1970, he is duplicated from the DNA of a prominent German political leader. That being said, Bobby has veered away from his "father's" ways and wishes to bring love joy to the burning man community.

Eric Hayes Live at Burning Man 2013

10587

Center Camp Cafe

The soulful conviction of Eric Hayes floods his audience with a hearty stew of rich tones and silky vibes. Even those whose thirst is never quenched cannot help but set down their drink, close their eyes and give in to the seductive musings of this rising star. Hailing from New Jersey, Eric Hayes is so much more than your all-American musician. His music possesses a stirring, earthy sound that leaves his fans aching for more. His voice is robust. His talent is pure. His passion is unmatched. The 31 year old Far Hills native and William Paterson University music graduate has been the recipient of several positive reviews by prestigious critics and has been featured in the Star Ledger, New York Village Voice Magazine, New York Post, the ASPCA and a host of online blogs and pop culture media sites. Hayes' credits include collaborating and performing with several big name artists such as Gavin Degraw, Martin Sexton, Bill Withers, Rusted Root, Indie artist Rachel Platten, Reggae legend Ziggy Marley and soul artist Joss Stone. 2013 has been and continues to be an incredible year for Hayes. He is truly humbled by the invitation to perform and share his music at Burning Man 2013 on the night the "Man Burns" for Black Rock City and such an incredible community of artists. Hayes is well known for his musical charity work and has headlined exclusive events held by some of the world’s most elite circles of hosts including the opening dinner ceremony for the United States Olympic Wrestling Team and headlining the internationally recognized American Giving Awards winning "More Than Me" charity. He is inspired by both male and female artists including Otis Redding, Sam Cooke, Miles Davis, Jimi Hendrix, Susan Tedeschi and Radio Head. Recently Hayes performed at the annual ASPCA fund raising charity event, attracting more than 15,000 people, during which he reportedly helped friend and animal advocate Prince Lorenzo Borghese raise more than $50,000 for animal welfare.

"So You Wanna Be A DJ" Shock Collar Gong Show

10679

Want It!

Have you always dreamed of throwing down a legendary DJ set at one of the hottest camps on the playa? Well, how bad do you Want It? We've got 10,000 watts of juicy sound, some of the best real estate in Black Rock City, and a nighttime crowd just waiting to be whipped into a frenzy. All you have to do is wow our panel of judges and you too could be headlining Burning Man! For this contest we hearken back to that seminal masterpiece of talent programs: The Gong Show. Perhaps you remember the cringe-worthy showcase of questionable performances that critics could halt by striking a loud gong. This event is eerily similar, only ours has balls. Ovaries too. Giant, dusty gonads. Can you hang? Instead of a gong, DJs will wear a shock collar and get buzzed off stage by volts of harsh rejection if they fail to impress. Instead of regaling us with tap dancing, DJs break out their most mind blowing tracks and slickest tricks. Instead of a paltry sum to commemorate victory, winners will be invited back during peak hours to pound the dance floor into submission. This is open decks for the fearless. Bring it.

11210

Dark Sparkle

Dark Sparkle is the potent mix of the mysterious and the dangerous that makes something irresistibly attractive. It's what pushes people to the point of insanity; that unexplainable quality that pulls people to the dark side. Some days, Dark Sparkle is your alter-ego; other days it is your most natural feeling form. Dark Sparkle is Mona Lisa's smile, biscuits and gravy, the Fonz, the apocalypse. It is an adventurous way of life--physically, emotionally and mentally that citizens of BRC embrace. Our shows are an opportunity for Dark Sparklers and other BRC citizens to explore and showcase their Dark Sparkle through performance, storytelling, and tease. MICRO dance performance (duet)

11974

MICRO

MICRO explores the small universe that is our body and mind. It consists of a 8ft x 12 ft x 8ft structure that has 200 translucent silicone balls hanging from the ceiling of the structure. When bumped into, each one lights up with one of 5 different colors as well as generating a unique sound. As people play with the balls they are engulfed by a symphony of lights and sounds surrounding them on all sides.

Dance your Thoughts into Transformation

11976

MICRO

That rare moment when we find deep quiet in the middle of our dance is rich. But what about the rest of the time? When our monkey mind is fully engaged, our thoughts dance in and among the embodied experience we are having. In this lab we will embrace our monkey mind and bring our soft focus to these thoughts. We will dip in and out of solos, duets, and group dances, taking time to reflect, journal, and discuss our mind's dance, and discover the pathway to underlying beliefs that hold these thought patterns in place. Once these are revealed, will we find commonality in our thought patterns? What will these beliefs point to regarding our lives off the dance floor?

Deep connections thru Dayburners and 7 Sunrises

11982

Camp Contact

Experiencing sunrises on the playa is beyond words can describe. While we can’t escape the loud dance music in the morning, NYC director/composer Charlie Dayburn composed a 7-track Original cinematic soundtrack to accompany dayburners like us who are seeking solitude at the dawn of the day. The 7 tracks express 7 roller coaster feelings throughout the week. Charlie Dayburn would like to share the whole album with fellow dayburners through 7 different connection exercises from body contact to soul gazing. This album is also tuned to 432Hz which believes it's the vibrational frequency of our human bodies. It's an more inward experience that is felt inside the body at the spine and heart. Each attendee will receive a copy of the album.

Embrace Pas de Deux

12017

Embrace

Conceived and choreographed to accompany the 'Embrace' sculpture, 'Embrace Pas de Deux' illustrates the act of falling in love as described through the art of classical and contemporary ballet. This eclectic dance piece explores the concept of accessing the Divine through romantic Love. It explores concepts of Divine Love by moving forward through history from Ancient Egypt, to the Classical period, and culminating in the present. The 25 minute piece includes audience lead group song and the sharing of personal intentions of Love. Embrace Pas de Deux features Sierra Nevada Ballet principal dancers Ananda Bena-Weber and Alexander Biber. The piece features the diverse choreographic styles of Rosine Bena, Horacio Cefuentes, and Ananda Bena-Weber.

SyneGy Live Open Jam Session

12115

Reverbia

For the 4th year straight, Reverbia has hosted SynerGy Live…the complete Black Rock City Jam Session Collective. SynerGy began its roots out of the Vancouver Burning Man Regional Festival scene, growing into a welcomed jam session of any and all who dare to create collective music. Drop in, glide for awhile, drop out. SynerGy is about the exchange and sharing of musical ideas. All musicians are invited to come jam in Reverbia's Embassy for one long set! Audience welcome to listen and dance to the spontaneous grooves, being created in the moment.

Autogenesis of the Brane

12136

Large Harmonic Collider...

Throughout the week, visitors to the Large Harmonic Collider camp will leave their personal interpretations of scientific inquiries, to be digested by the Brane, a spatiotemporal geodome artifact synthesizing wind, light, sound and thought. Experience an Autogenesis of the Brane, where we will interpret the musings of Burners, guide a sonic/visual performance of the Brane's language with strings and percussion, and complete an autogenic training with the Cosmic Rain Game, making music with our bodies and watching the lights react.

Jewish Motherly Advice

12263

Children of Chaos

Lisa Schroeder of the Children of Chaos will be hosting her Jewish Mother booth again this year, dispensing advice and nurturing for all. “The Jewish Mother You Never Had” will be available daily and Mom's hours will be posted in front of the camp. Mama Lisa will be providing cookies, milk, (maybe even a bagel!) and lots of love and caring for Burners requiring a little TLC - in English, Hebrew, Yiddish, French, and/or Spanish. The 2009 version of this event won the Acculturation Video award from Burning Man (http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dtX8Z-izffs\). As Mama Lisa says, "everyone needs motherly advice, but who wants to hear if from their own mother?...oy, too much baggage!" Come visit with Burning Man's very own Jewish Mother who dispenses love, nurturing, advice and no guilt (unless absolutely necessary).

LNTV – Environmental Movies on the Playa

Earth Guardians

Will technology save us, or is it up to us to take the steps necessary to change our world, not to save our planet, but to save ourselves. Kostume Gifting Experience

12401

Kostume Kult

Let Kostume Kult transform you with a new costume or accessory! Costume experts dress you & send you dancing down the runway. Silliness guaranteed. Kostume Kult recreates the glory days of NYC circa the 1970's by transporting you to the seedy throwback replica of "Times Square BRC". The Empire State Building and 25ft King Kong loom above the NYC skyline while a runway show that blows fashion week out of the dust goes on street level starring you. As a premiere daytime destination, Kostume Kult will be providing costume transformations to the under-accessorized masses of BRC. No person shall go uncostumed or unfabulous because we have a full team of costume stylists ready to dress you up and help you transform. The only thing we ask of you is a proud strut down our runway to display your new duds to booty moving music. If you prefer a DIY approach, step inside our Krafting Dome where you can gain the supplies and know-how to upgrade your bike and your look. Our professional staff knows their way around a glue gun and we're not afraid to bedazzle YOU! The playa provides the grit, we supply the glamour so hop the K Train to costume transformations, music and a non stop runway show that would make RuPaul blush. Of course the city never sleeps and our amazing DJ line up keeps us moving into the night as the city lights shine bright into the dark playa night. Also not to be missed is the Peepshow FreaKKshow, BRC's only 24 hour participatory peep show where you can be the star or simply sneak a peek at some Big Apples! Down our alleys you will find costumes, crafting, sparkle pony vagrants, playa hustlers, burner working gals and street wise tramps. You won't want to miss it so jump the turnstile to the KKrossroads Of The World. After all if you can make it here you can make it anywhere!

Dawn of the Burning Sun concert

12488

Black Rock Observatory

Experiencing the divine and magical sunrises on the playa is beyond words can describe. While we can’t escape the loud dance music in the morning, many dayburners (burners who are more focus on the daytime activities) are seeking solitude at the dawn of the day. NYC director/composer Dayburn (Charlie Wan) will be performing his original cinematic score at Black Rock Observatory (designed by 2013 Temple designer Gregg Fleishman) to accompany your deep connecting moment with the most important star in our universe - the Sun. There will be live visual projection of the sun from solar telescope by astrophysicist Matt O'Dowd. Any art cars with sound systems and FM radio receivers are welcomed to participate our additional immersive simulcast soundscape experience. There will be a small numbers of radio receivers available to be borrowed at the event. The concert starts at the first ray of light on friday morning (August 29, 6am). Bring your open heart and look to the east.

Funk and fashion: A Soul Evolution Soirée

12507

Salon Soleil

Title: Funk and fashion: A Soul Evolution Soirée In the tarot, each individual soul is represented by the The Fool. We are all Fools in the journey we call life. The 22 major arcana cards represent the different stages of evolution we all encounter on our way to seeking enlightenment. Join us for this very special, tarot themed fashion show as Pouncy takes you on this journey of soul evolution seeking enlightenment, visually displayed though burner fashions. Following the show, get your groove on with some funk-tified frequencies that will have you vibrating in the higher realms.

Starry Starry Night, Black Rock City

12514

Up in the skies

During Burning Man 2013 I looked up at the sky on Wednesday night and saw only the very brightest of stars with the great majority of them washed out by the lights of our city in the desert. I contrasted this in my mind with the first year I came to the play and "Instead of going to sleep I sat in the door of my tent and just let the glorious light of ALL THOSE STARS wash over me. I could hold my hand out and see a clear shadow on the cracked and fizzured playa, from the stars alone." Our art project for Burning Man 2014 will be to enlist the active cooperation of approximately 68 thousand other burners as "co-artists" with Creation to turn every non-essential light in the city OFF for two hours on the night of Wednesday, August 27th from 11pm to 1am on the 28th. Then, everyone can look up and share with me the wonder of our sky there at Black Rock City which most have never seen. To borrow a phrase we'll all be able to "take a trip and never leave the farm." We may not succeed fully or at all but it's fun and cheap to try : ).

Living Theatre, The

The Living Theatre is curating a one week revolutionary theatre festival within the festival. Presenting everything from live performances to workshops. ceciNESTpas

12692

ceciNESTpas

ceciNESTpas is a nest of 10 meters diameter built by vultures that will invite and welcome wandering travelers. Inside it all around the nest structure are arranged illustrated board of the history of The Jungle Book. The nest will prove to visitor to be a jungle to cross. So while you progress through the story you advance into the jungle to get out at the end of the story. The artist Francesca Nini Carbonini constructs in these illustrations a comparison between the jungle of Kipling with our modern jungle, telling the abandonment in the jungles that over time inexorably become a familiar place in which the individual abandoned finds himself and creates its warm nest, but… ceciNESTpas!

Monster in a Box

12880

Conception

An interactive art installation, fashioned when traders going east on the Slick Route were stalked by a devious, bloodthirsty creature that uses sound mimicry to lure in its victims. After killing several members of the party the monster was captured and is being brought back to civilization to be sold as a curiosity. Participants will be drawn to the crate by plaintive human or animal cries of distress. Once its victim is close by, the monster will thrash hungrily from inside the crate and give off blood curdling screams.

The Unchurch Service

13077

Chakralicious Camp

This is a theatrical performance contrasting religion and spirituality throughout history, and showing how atheists and theists need each other to avoid the pitfalls of religious fundamentalism. The spirituality embedded in religious texts is universal and profound, and has been of great benefit to society, but the undisciplined psychology of human beings leads to its oversimplification and use as a tool to control others. Atheists today are in a unique position to support critical thinking within a religious society that often condemns it.

CARYATID

13169

Campsite TBD

This action art work utilizes BUTOH-inspired movement to envision an inert, architectural column, carved in the shape of a woman, come to life. Three sound tracks demonstrate the Kuleshov effect. Viewers will discover various interpretations of the movement with three different soundtracks, or observe the piece utilizing the haptic, environmental soundscape of the performance space. This short piece is structured in three parts. The first part serves as an awakening, as the caryatid discovers movement from the perch of the entablature onto which it is mounted. The second part captures the caryatid’s realization of increased mobility, and the expansion of its sensate environment. The third part chronicles the caryatid’s awareness of its limitations, and the slow recognition of its inevitable embrace back to its native form. Choreographed by Hortense Gerardo Produced by in vivo Productions

SlaveMart at the Souk

13269

Santa Cruz: Slave Mart

Enjoy tea of a dubious nature, become a slave for an hour or just watch the event! SlaveMart is an interactive performance piece that celebrates the little known 11th Principle, “Radical Self Enslavement” (sometimes known as DIY Brainwashing). One can relax at our Tea and Slaves Shoppe and have some teas of a dubious nature while being served by beautiful slave drivers. When the time is right ten lucky volunteer enslavees will be marched up to the cat walk and be auctioned off. But this is no ordinary auction. In this one, the merchandise is king and can pick and choose among the myriad offers of the crowd below. Bids can be a ride in an art car, foot massage or perhaps the best martini on the playa. When a suitable exchange has been agreed upon the slightly deranged Auctioneer hammers the bid to a close and Slaver and Slavee go off on a one-hour adventure that is mutually enjoyable for both. And both get necklaces to boot.

Wrestling Exhibition in honor of Hanuman

13930

Sun Guardians

We are exploring an exhibition / fun event in the temple on Thursday for a wrestling event Indian Style (East Indian called Kushti). But any kind of wrestling in an inflated rubber tub filled with mud. Wrestlers are welcome to wear a traditional wrap, speedo, shorts or ...nothing. This is for fun and not to be taken too seriously. An official and first aide person will be present. Participants can be any gender and an audience will surround the tub and are encouraged to bring playa gifts for the winners. Reward your warriors. WANT TO PARTICIPATE? Stay engaged here on this event. If you want to camp with Sun Guardians follow the links in the about section. We are exploring the idea and encouraging people to come join in on the fun as a participant! Audience or Wrestler... come have fun and tell us what you think.

Hechi-Ken Hamazaki / Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD

13964

Venus Lift - Mega Mikos...

The art performance by Japanese contemporary artist, Ken Hamazaki. This performance was inspired by and arranged from the Japanese traditional tea ceremony. I named myself Hechi-Ken after the legendary master of tea ceremony, Hechi-Kan. The original ceremony consists of a variety of manners to drink, but to experience this fully, please simply drink with a style you favor most. The most interesting practice would be turning your thought toward him for a few minutes without speaking and enjoy drinking in this small silent space. I always serve this tea for whoever sits down in front of me. Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- is always a great tool to communicate universally without any thought of hierarchy. I'll be happy if we could find any great idea to make better and more enjoyable future throughout this tea ceremony.

Dark Sparkle Burlesque Extravaganza

14294

Dark Sparkle

Dark Sparkle is the potent mix of the mysterious and the dangerous that makes something irresistibly attractive. It's what pushes people to the point of insanity; that unexplainable quality that pulls people to the dark side. Some days, Dark Sparkle is your alter-ego; other days it is your most natural feeling form. Dark Sparkle is Mona Lisa's smile, biscuits and gravy, the Fonz, the apocalypse. It is an adventurous way of life--physically, emotionally and mentally that citizens of BRC embrace. Our shows are an opportunity for Dark Sparklers and other BRC citizens to explore and showcase their Dark Sparkle through performance, storytelling, and tease. Featuring your favorite DS performers as well as guests from the BRC community. We'll also turn the tables with ample opportunity for participation. Contact: srodenburg@gmail.com

CelloJoe records live on stage with a loop pedal and produces intricate tapestries of harmony, melody, and rhythm. Eye of Argon - Comedy Reading/Group Performance

15070

Silicon Village

Greetings mortals, welcome to the world of Grignr the mightiest of barbarians. Come and join us on the Silicon Village stage for a group reading of the funniest and most terrible pieces of fan fiction ever produced... 'The Eye of Argon." Bear witness to the near impossible to read dialogue without bursting into laughter as other readers and members of the audience act out the scenes from this story regardless of inconsistencies, spelling errors, grammar errors, capitalization errors, tense errors, and made up words that make no sense! Do you have the stomach for dialogue such as this? "The vile stench of the Shaman's hot fetid breath over came the nauseated female with a deep soul searing sickness, causing her to wrench her head backwards and regurgitate a slimy, orange white stream of swelling gore over the richly woven purple robe of the enthused acolyte." If so come to the reading of the "Eye of Argon" written 35 years ago and has yet to be forgotten in the sands of time. The dialogue may seem impossible, but the terrible show will go on!
