The 48 Hour Film Project: Black Rock City 2015

15818

Videogasm

Camp Videogasm will again be host to The Black Rock City edition of The 48 Hour Film Project. Were groups of burners write, shoot and edit films over a 48 hour period while at Burning Man to be shown at Videogasm on Thursday night (9/3) at 11pm. We'll start with a retrospective of short films produced at Burning Man in previous years and then premiere the videos that will be produced at this year's Burning Man! Filmmakers: If you have a team and equipment, start at your leisure and follow the instructions on posters found at PlayaInfo and Videogasm (in Snowflake Village). Lust & Marriage: A Woman's Journey into Polyamory

15994

Sacred Spaces Village

From the opening moments, we learn this solo show is about soul mates, and the search for love and lust. Emily is the hero of the story, a character very much a literary stand-in for author and performer Eleanor O’Brien. We meet her as a child, fascinated by romance novels and her father’s porn. The show traces her journey from awkward teen to college boyfriends, complete with disappointing first times and disastrous blowjobs. But then she discovers renown sex-columnist Dan Savage, her ‘gay fairy godfather’. Dan helps her learn to ask for what she wants (“I can touch my own clit during sex?”), and encourages her to be GGG (Good, Giving and Game). Emily goes on a spree of experimentation, culminating in the “grand prix of getting lucky,” Burning Man. At the world’s largest alternative event, she meets Matt, who turns out to be the love of her life-but he doesn’t identify as monogamous. Can they make it work? Emily asks Dan for advice as they navigate the thrills and valleys of opening the relationship: how to negotiate boundaries, deal with jealousy and keep from falling in love with other people. She thinks if they follow the rules they've set, they can keep their relationship safe. They can be “monogamish,” and keep the spark in their marriage. When a magical threesome drives her to utter meltdown, Emily insists on closing their marriage. But monogamy doesn’t solve all their problems. Emily and Matt discover they have different libidos - and the seven-year itch isn’t a myth. He encourages her to spread her wings, so she takes a lover. All's fine for a while, but soon she finds herself falling in love with Michael, her NSA partner for play. She is terrified of losing her marriage to Matt, and asks Dan again for advice. “Is polyamory a utopian ideal?” During an ayahuasca ceremony, Emily finally sees where she's been blind to how her behavior has stifled her marriage, and how she has to let go of the need for certainty, or controlling anyone else’s heart.

SORNE at Burning Man 2015

17084

DUSTFISH Village

Morgan Sorne, known in his solo music project as SORNE, is an American singer-songwriter, composer, multi-media artist, music producer, and actor. He is known for his supernatural vocal range and utilization of homemade instruments and found sounds to create sonic tapestries of layered vocal samples and unconventional instrumentation. His performances often feature an construct of self-made visual art pieces inspired by personal and cultural archetypes, a continual thread woven throughout his performance aesthetic. SORNE performs and tours with a revolving cast of dancers, musicians and artists while working with local communities of peoples around the world to create unique participatory live experiences of his work, thus blurring the line between performer and audience member. His musical style has been described as a combination of tribal, electronica, avant-garde, avant pop, alternative rock, and opera.

Ayla Nereo sunrise set @ Camp Mystic

17171

Camp Mystic

THURS morning at 6:30 AM ~ Join Ayla at Camp Mystic to sing in the wildness of the heart and greet the dawning sun. With an array of loop-pedals by her side, she builds layer upon layer of vocal melodies into fierce, sweeping harmonies and weaves syncopated threads of guitar, kalimba, piano, and percussion into each live performance. Her lucid storytelling and lyrical imagery are water for the thirsty soul; words and sounds that crack open the heart, and embody the many folds of our own selves. ACTOROKE at Camp Baggage Check'

18137

Baggage Check

Actoroke is “Karaoke for actors.” In Karaoke you would pick a song to sing in front of your friends and strangers. In Actoroke, you and a friend pick a scene from a popular movie to act out. We will have a full film crew setup, complete with 3 cameras (wide master, and one on each actor), wireless lapel mics for each actor, 2 teleprompters (one for each actor, in their eye line), and a truss and lighting setup. You will be directed by our camp’s filmmaker, Hoss Hitchcock, who will help you through your performance. Come get the full experience of acting and being directed. The video feeds from all three cameras will be displayed in the “video village” where your friends and strangers can watch your performance! If this sounds fun but you don’t want to act, then try your hand at running a camera or teleprompter! Wed & Fri 10:00 pm to late

Movie Mirror Camera Obscura by Liminal Labs

19708

Liminal Labs

Liminal Labs Workshop is fustian to announce a breakthrough advance in the art of Camera Obscura. Utilizing our Movie Mirror Obscura technology, what wast once restricted to the dark isolation of a head-sized box or a stuffy, lightless chamber, is anon a shared, open-air experience under the stars themselves. Thrill to see actual, illuminate images of people, places, and things (things!!!) that seem to move with a divine direction of their own making. Leonardo daVinci was himself taken with the possibilities of the Camera Obscura. Inspired, Liminal Labs Workshop does the Master one better by adding focused, intense illumination on a 53-foot white wall to offer an experience beyond what even Leonardo might imagine. Indeed, the Movie Mirror Obscura dual screen system shines brighter than the heavens and is blended with sounds to tempt the dancing angels. From Tuesda through Friday, each evening’s dark of night brings, not one, but two images magically mirrored, side-by-side for thy Royal amusement. Prithee shaketh thy booty if so moved. Or sit and enjoy the movie magic.

Hechi-Ken Hamazaki / Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD

19753

Wrongtown

Art performance by Japanese contemporary artist, Ken Hamazaki. This performance was inspired by and arranged from traditional Japanese tea ceremony. The original ceremony consists of a variety of manners to drink, but to experience this fully, please simply drink with a style you favor most. The most interesting practice would be turning your thoughts inward for a few minutes without speaking and enjoy drinking in this small silent space. I always serve this tea for whoever sits down in front of me. Red Tea Ceremony -YOU ARE GOD- is always a great tool to communicate universally without any thought of hierarchy. I'll be happy if we could find any great idea to make a brighter, better, and more enjoyable future through this tea ceremony.

Shamans of the Global Village - Film Screening

20181

Red Lightning

Indigenous people across the globe have used sacred plant medicines for millennia to heal, illuminate and connect them to the web of life. Each of these psychoactive medicines needs a healer to connect them to their patients: the shaman. This investigative-adventure documentary show examines not just these shamanic medicines, but the shamans that wield them. If, as Marshall McLuhan said, we are now a “global village”, then we need our own healers that understand the deep power and sacredness these plant medicines can reveal. Film screening followed by Filmmakers Q&A session.

Reverbia Interactive Live Music Art Wall Mural

20198

Reverbia

Reverbia presents for the first time our Reverbia Interactive Live Music Art Wall Mural! As our Live Music resonates through your ears, share your depths of perspective and emotion through the iterative expression of Art Wall Painting. Noted Canadian artist Danielle Caners, leads an expedition into the realms of unknown, improvised art, where only through the collective creative mind, can a masterpiece be discovered. Daily and nightly, when the live music is playing, come share your artistic expression by painting upon our mural canvas wall. Portions of Reverbia's Art Wall Mural will be painting between established lines, while other areas of the Art Wall Mural will be free formed expression. *Note that the Reverbia Art Wall Mural will not be open 24 hours…but will operate throughout the day and night whenever our artist supervision is available. During Reverbia's concerts in the Shade Series and Reverbia Live Nights…the Art Wall Mural will be the most consistently available for public painting and expression.

48 Hour Film Project: Black Rock City

20244

Videogasm

Videogasm will again be host to The Black Rock City edition of The 48 Hour Film Project. Were groups of burners write, shoot and edit films over a 48 hour period to be shown at a festival on Thursday night. We'll start with a retrospective of short films produced at Burning Man in previous years and then premiere the shorts that will be produced at this years Burning Man! Filmmakers: If you have a team and equipment, start at your leisure and follow the instructions on posters found at PlayaInfo and Videogasm (in Snowflake Village). If you're looking to form a team come to Videogasm at 3pm on Tuesday (8/30) to meet up with other like minded individuals. Film's should be under 10 minutes in length, contain the three ingredients (character, prop & line of dialog) listed on the posters mentioned above, and be brought to Videogasm by 8pm on Thursday (9/1). You can now shoot and edit a film on your smart phone, so get out there and make a film!

WE: Web of experiences

20303

Champagne Chandeliers

The WEB OF EXPERIENCES (WE) is a web of ropes and light strings that invites all passers-by to share a piece of themselves--knowledge, art, thoughts, or an experience. All passers-by and visitors will feel inspired (and be asked) to contribute to WE by writing, drawing or creating on individual (cloth grommet-lined moop-proof) flags which will be attached to WE. Throughout the week, WE will organically grow and participants can walk amongst and be inspired by this hanging garden that signifies BRC’s collective, shared wisdom. Some pieces in WE will be written in mirror cursive, a homage to Da Vinci’s notebooks--we will provide pocket mirrors to decipher their meaning.

2016 Black Rock City Air Guitar Championship

20607

FreeStyle Palace

2016 Black Rock City Air Guitar Championship - Esplanade & 6:45 OFFICIAL RULES OF COMPETITION: Each performance is played to 1 minute (60 sec.) of a song The 60 second song will be provided to you from a list of 100+ tracks to choose from The instrument must be invisible & be a guitar, i.e. air drums not allowed Air roadies are allowed, but must leave the stage before the performance Back-up bands (air or real) are not allowed Black Rock City Air Guitar contests each consist of two rounds: Round 1 (freestyle): each competitor performs to a song of their choice from the list Round 2 (compulsory): top competitors from round 1 perform surprise song JUDGING CRITERIA: The jury is a panel of independent judges. The results of the jury cannot be protested. All performances are scored on a scale from 4.0 to 6.0 – 6.0 being the highest possible. Scores are given to one decimal point (e.g. 5.4, not 5.48). A single score is given to each air guitarist based on their overall performance in that round. The score reflects the quality of the performance based on three key criteria: 1. Technical merit - You don’t have to know what notes you’re playing, but the more your invisible fretwork corresponds to the music that’s playing, the better the performance. 2. Stage presence - Anyone can do it in the privacy of their bedroom. Few have what it takes to rock a crowd of hundreds or even thousands – all without an instrument. 3. “Airness” - The last criteria is the most difficult to define yet often the most decisive of all. Airness is defined as the extent to which a performance transcends the imitation of a real guitar and becomes an art form in and of itself. Please note: the scores from BOTH ROUNDS are added to determine the contestants’ final scores. This combined score determines the winner. Earn the title of Black Rock City Air Guitar Champion!

Symbiogenesis: Evolution & future biology of Earth

20834

Center Camp Cafe

Symbiogenesis is the process by which groups of organisms merge into more complex meta-organisms. It is the process that lead to the evolution of complex cells and all macroscopic life. As a pattern, Symbiogenesis points the way to how we might design a human civilization that is so interconnected with other livings organisms that our buildings and cities become living, breathing, reproducing meta-organisms themselves, ushering in a new age in the evolution of the world-body.

Gonzo Communications: Hunter Thompson & Activism

20920

Center Camp Cafe

Based on the book "Dear Dr. Thompson: Felony Murder, Hunter S. Thompson and the Last Gonzo Campaign" about my work with gonzo journalist Hunter S. Thompson to free a young woman from prison for a crime she obviously did not commit. This talk illuminates another side of the author as an activist--not about the guns and drugs. This is an educational talk about why America should abolish the Felony Murder statue which can hold people accountable for crimes they had no intention of committing. But most importantly it is about the lessons I learned from Hunter Thompson as his colleague and how a simple letter can change a person's life.

Is Burning Man Gentrifying

21164

Center Camp Cafe

For the past four years, the BRC Census has reported a steady rise in the median income of Burners which is significantly faster than the rate of inflation. This led some of us to wonder whether Burning Man was "gentrifying" to some degree; becoming less inclusive of low-income participants due to cost or other factors. We hope to present data and discuss conclusions from what we know thus far.
